# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:45:12.555054

### Base Program

```py
def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def countPartitions(nums, k):
    total_sum = sum(nums)
    n = len(nums)
    mod = 1000000007

    if total_sum < k * 2:
        return 0

    dp = [1] * (n + 1)

    for i in range(1, k):
        for j in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
            dp[j] = (dp[j] * j + dp[j - 1]) % mod

    result = 0

    for i in range(n - 1):
        total_sum -= nums[i]
        if total_sum >= k:
            result = (result + dp[i + 1]) % mod

    return result


```
